        <h1 class="header heading fr">Should I convert dollars to pounds before I leave us - London Forum</h1> 
        <!--trkP:trip_planner_breadcrumbs--> 
        <!-- PLACEMENT trip_planner_breadcrumbs -->

           <span class="ui_button_overlay" style="float:right"> <span class="saves-widget-button ui_button small saves secondary save-post-57784692" data-type="post" data-id="57784692" data-icon-class="red-heart" data-title="Should I convert dollars to pounds before I leave us" data-text-saved="Reply Saved" data-text="Save Reply" data-params="geo=186338,forum_id=17,topic_id=7397278" onclick="return remoteModule(event, this);" data-load-all="stat-modal" data-load-dust="styleguide" data-load-init="saves/views/stat_modal/SaveApps.start"> <span class="ui_icon red-heart saves-icon-locator"></span> <span class="saves-text-locator">Save Reply</span> </span> <span class="btnoverlay loading"><span class="bubbles small"><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></span> </span> 
           <div class="postTitle"> 
            <span class="postNum">2.</span> 
            <span class="titleText"> Re: Should I convert dollars to pounds before I leave us </span> 
           </div> 
           <div class="postDate">

           </div> 
           <div class="postBody"> 
            <div id="pst_adm_57784692"></div> 
            <div id="top_adm_7397278"></div> 
            <div id="usr_adm_LauraRW"></div> 
            <p>If you want, you can get a few, but don't come with too much.</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>Use your ATM card to withdraw s instead--check with your bank to see if it has any relationship with banks in the UK. Let them, and your credit card company know of your travels, so your cards won't be frozen for fraud.</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>Carry only the cash you need for the day. Use ATMs to withdraw it. Pay for hotel and such with credit card.</p> 
           </div> 
          </div>

            <div id="usr_adm_Peterscot"></div> 
            <p>Theres many similar questions onhere, so you could read older posts and gain knowledge.</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>Generally, it can be cheaper to take out money of ATMs, using a card connected to your account. But YOU need to check what your bank cgarges fir this, and what rates money cgangers in the US give you.</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>Use cash for small purchases/expenses, and use credit cards for larger spends.</p>

           <span class="ui_button_overlay" style="float:right"> <span class="saves-widget-button ui_button small saves secondary save-post-57791445" data-type="post" data-id="57791445" data-icon-class="red-heart" data-title="Should I convert dollars to pounds before I leave us" data-text-saved="Reply Saved" data-text="Save Reply" data-params="geo=186338,forum_id=17,topic_id=7397278" onclick="return remoteModule(event, this);" data-load-all="stat-modal" data-load-dust="styleguide" data-load-init="saves/views/stat_modal/SaveApps.start"> <span class="ui_icon red-heart saves-icon-locator"></span> <span class="saves-text-locator">Save Reply</span> </span> <span class="btnoverlay loading"><span class="bubbles small"><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></span> </span>

            <div id="pst_adm_57791445"></div> 
            <div id="top_adm_7397278"></div> 
            <div id="usr_adm_flannan"></div> 
            <p>Agree with Leagle. Having £100 in your pocket relieves the hassle of finding an ATM when you deplane. Look online for the best price to purchase, will probably be a batter rate than ordering through your bank.</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>After that, it's all ATMs and credit cards. Contact your bank with your travel dates and ask if they have a 'partner'bank in the UK, who's withdrawal fees will be cheaper than just using any random ATM.</p> 
            <small>Edited: 25 April 2014, 00:19</small> 
           </div>

           <span class="ui_button_overlay" style="float:right"> <span class="saves-widget-button ui_button small saves secondary save-post-57791806" data-type="post" data-id="57791806" data-icon-class="red-heart" data-title="Should I convert dollars to pounds before I leave us" data-text-saved="Reply Saved" data-text="Save Reply" data-params="geo=186338,forum_id=17,topic_id=7397278" onclick="return remoteModule(event, this);" data-load-all="stat-modal" data-load-dust="styleguide" data-load-init="saves/views/stat_modal/SaveApps.start"> <span class="ui_icon red-heart saves-icon-locator"></span> <span class="saves-text-locator">Save Reply</span> </span> <span class="btnoverlay loading"><span class="bubbles small"><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></span> </span> 
           <div class="postTitle"> 
            <span class="postNum">9.</span> 
            <span class="titleText"> Re: Should I convert dollars to pounds before I leave us </span> 
           </div> 
           <div class="postDate">
            25 April 2014, 00:44
           </div> 
           <div class="postBody"> 
            <div id="pst_adm_57791806"></div> 
            <div id="top_adm_7397278"></div> 
            <div id="usr_adm_hoogo"></div> 
            <p>US residents normally get the best rates using an ATM. Should you decide to buy some UK currency in the USA, you are unlikely to find anywhere cheaper than a Wells Fargo International Teller site. You have one in Delray Beach.</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>PLAZA AT DELRAY</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>1500 S FEDERAL HWY</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>DELRAY BEACH, FL 33483</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>Call to confirm currency availability:</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>5612721501 </p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external" target="_blank" href="https://www.foreignexchangeservices.com/index.html?partnerid=FES&amp;serviceType=stores">https:/…</a></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>Today's markup was only 4.4%, usually it is a bit over 5%. I believe that Wells Fargo changes the rates just once per day. </p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>£100 would cost $175.43 at Wells Fargo.</p> 
            <p></p> 
            <p>Warning! £100 would cost $204.12 at a Travelex office in a US airport. (21.4% markup!)</p> 
           </div>

           <span class="ui_button_overlay" style="float:right"> <span class="saves-widget-button ui_button small saves secondary save-post-57797579" data-type="post" data-id="57797579" data-icon-class="red-heart" data-title="Should I convert dollars to pounds before I leave us" data-text-saved="Reply Saved" data-text="Save Reply" data-params="geo=186338,forum_id=17,topic_id=7397278" onclick="return remoteModule(event, this);" data-load-all="stat-modal" data-load-dust="styleguide" data-load-init="saves/views/stat_modal/SaveApps.start"> <span class="ui_icon red-heart saves-icon-locator"></span> <span class="saves-text-locator">Save Reply</span> </span> <span class="btnoverlay loading"><span class="bubbles small"><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></span> </span> 
           <div class="postTitle"> 
            <span class="postNum">10.</span> 
            <span class="titleText"> Re: Should I convert dollars to pounds before I leave us </span>

           <div class="postBody"> 
            <div id="pst_adm_57797579"></div> 
            <div id="top_adm_7397278"></div> 
            <div id="usr_adm_Waterwoman10"></div> 
            <p>I tried to buy online (75-100 pounds) and because they have a minimum of 200 dollars for a sale, plus a 15 dollar fee, as I recall, I didn't use Wells Fargo or any other online service. My bank's rates that day were high, so with their fee and exchange rate it still cost me 150.00 US dollars to get 75 pounds (for a booked car from Heathrow when I book and a little extra). But that was better than being forced to get more pounds at that rate. No Wells Fargo physical International Teller site where I live-hopefully you can get whatever amount you want from them.</p> 
           </div>

require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {
var define = widgets.define.bind(widgets,'homepage_tripadvisor_footer_links','handlers',['deferred/HelpCenterOverlay','handlers']);
define([
"widget", 'lib/jquery-amd',
"ta/util/Cookie", 'ta/util/ActionRecord'
], function(
widget, $,
taCookie, Track
) {
'use strict';
// called onclick by the wrapper div
function _checkForPid(event) {
var target = event ? (event.srcElement || event.target) : null;
if (target && target.getAttribute("data-pid")) {
taCookie.setPIDCookie(target.getAttribute("data-pid"));
}
}
$(widget.element).on("click", '.js_click[data-id="help_center"]', function(){
var el = this;
var url = $(el).data('url');
widget.require(['trjs!deferred/HelpCenterOverlay', 'trcss!src/build/required/help_center_overlay'], function(o) {
o.open(el, url);
});
});
$(widget.element).on("click", ".footerLink", function(event) {
var actionPrefix = "Footer_";
var link = $(this);
var action = link.data('trackAction');
if (!action) {
return;
}
var opensNewWindow = ("_blank" == link.attr("target"));
if (link.is("a") && !opensNewWindow) {
event.preventDefault();
Track.record(actionPrefix + action)
.always(function() {
window.location = link.attr("href");
});
} else {
Track.record(actionPrefix + action);
}
});
return {
checkForPid : _checkForPid
};
});

define("cpm/AdBlockDetect", ["lib/jquery-amd","utils/browserutils","ta/Core/TA.Event","ta/Core/TA.Record","ta/util/Error"],
function( $, Browser, taEvent, taRecord, taError) {
'use strict';
var exports = {};
var _logged = false;
var _cdn = window.CDNHOST || "";
var _pixelUrl = "/img2/x.gif?&ads=1&adsize=2&adslot=3&rnd=";
var _generatePixel = function() {
var rnd = Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000);
return $('<img src="' + _cdn + _pixelUrl + rnd + '" class="ad ad_column" height="0" width="0" />');
};
var _log = function(blocked, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked){
if (!_logged && trackingLabel){
if (blocked || trackUnblocked) {
taRecord.trackEventOnPage(trackingLabel, Browser.name, blocked, 0, false);
}
_logged = true;
}
};
var _detect = function(testImg, onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked){
if (testImg){
var blocked = !testImg[0].offsetParent;
_log(blocked, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked);
if (blocked) {
onDetectedHandler();
}
}
};
exports.runIfDetected = function(onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked) {
if ( typeof onDetectedHandler != "function") {
taError.record(null, "runIfDetected requires a function");
return;
}
taEvent.queueForLoad( function() {
_logged = false;
var testImg = _generatePixel();
testImg.on("load", function(){ _detect(testImg, onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked); });
testImg.on("error", function(){ _detect(testImg, onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked); });
$("body").append(testImg);
}, "AdBlockDetect");
};
return exports;
});

define('common/Radio', ['vanillajs'], function(){
var RADIOS = {};
var SPLITTER = /\s+/;
function Radio(channel){
this.channel = channel;
this.events = {};
this.replies = {};
}
Radio.prototype.reply = function(name, callback, context){
name.split(SPLITTER).forEach(function(n){
this.replies[n] || (this.replies[n] = []);
this.replies[n].push({
callback: callback,
context: context || this
});
}, this);
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.request = function(name){
if (!this.replies[name]){ return null; }
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
var r = this.replies[name];
r = r[r.length - 1];
return r.callback.apply(r.context, args);
};
Radio.prototype.requestMany = function(name){
if (!this.replies[name]){ return null; }
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
return this.replies[name].map(function(r){
return r.callback.apply(r.context, args);
});
};
Radio.prototype.requestAll = function(name, expected){
if (!this.replies[name]){ return true; }
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
var fn = typeof expected == 'function' ? expected : function(v){ return v === expected; };
return this.replies[name].reduce(function(b, r){
return b && fn(r.callback.apply(r.context, args));
}, true);
};
Radio.prototype.requestEvery = Radio.prototype.requestAll;
Radio.prototype.requestAny = function(name, expected){
if (!this.replies[name]){ return false; }
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
var fn = typeof expected == 'function' ? expected : function(v){ return v === expected; };
return this.replies[name].reduce(function(b, r){
return b || fn(r.callback.apply(r.context, args));
}, false);
};
Radio.prototype.requestSome = Radio.prototype.requestAny;
Radio.prototype.on = function(name, callback, context){
name.split(SPLITTER).forEach(function(n){
this.events[n] || (this.events[n] = []);
this.events[n].push({
callback: callback,
context: context || this
});
}, this);
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.once = function(name, callback, context){
name.split(SPLITTER).forEach(function(n){
this.events[n] || (this.events[n] = []);
this.events[n].push({
callback: callback,
context: context || this,
single: true
});
}, this);
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.one = Radio.prototype.once;
Radio.prototype.off = function(name, callback){
name.split(SPLITTER).forEach(function(n){
if (!this.events[n]) {return;}
this.events[n] = this.events[n].filter(function(o){
return callback && o.callback != callback;
});
}, this);
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.trigger = function(name){
if (!this.events[name]) {return;}
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
this.events[name] = this.events[name].filter(function(o){
o.callback.apply(o.callback, args);
return !o.single;
});
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.emit = Radio.prototype.trigger;
return function(channel){
return (RADIOS[channel] || (RADIOS[channel] = new Radio(channel)));
};
});
require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {

define([
'placement',
'lib/jquery-amd',
'common/Radio'
], function(
placement,
$,
Radio
) {

openMyTrips(false, true);
});
// Update Global Nav content
var _onSuccessLoginRefresh = (function(response) {
window.userLoggedIn = true;
// Update the masthead, but keep some of the old content.
// This is because the AJAX servlet does not generate the correct content
// for the original page (instead, it generates it for /MetaPlacementAjax).
// Note this uses the IDs to match each "old" element with its corresponding "new" element.
var oldMenus = $("<div>").append(placementEl.find('.global-nav-no-refresh'));
placementEl.html(response);
placementEl.find('.global-nav-no-refresh').each(function(idx, el) {
$(el).replaceWith(oldMenus.find('#' + el.getAttribute('id'))[0]);
});
if (oldOverlay) {
oldOverlay.hide('replace-el');
}
}).bind(placementEl);
var _getRequestOptionsForLoginRefresh = function() {
return {
// This should not be necessary, but for some reason placements
// seems tightly coupled with the location store
skipLocation: placement.location_id <= 0,
returnTo: document.location.pathname + (document.location.search||'') + (document.location.hash||'')
};
};
// When login state changes, request the updated global nav
$(document).on('regOverlay:success', function() {
placement.requestAJAXPlacement( _onSuccessLoginRefresh, null, _getRequestOptionsForLoginRefresh());
});
// When mousing over the global nav links, show their submenus
placementEl.on('mouseenter', '.global-nav-links-container [data-element]', function(evt) {
var elmt = $(this);

if (oldOverlay) {
oldOverlay.hide('new-overlay');
}
// Is there a submenu to show?
var menuEl = placementEl.find(elmt.data('element')).clone();
if (!menuEl.length) {
return;
}
var reqs = ['trjs!overlays/Overlay',
'trjs!overlays/styles/flyout',
'trjs!overlays/options/closeOnMouseAway',
'trjs!overlays/position',
'trjs!overlays/options/destroyOnHide'
];

var overlay = new Overlay(elmt[0], new Flyout(menuEl[0], 'global-nav-flyout global-nav-menu'), CloseOnMouseAway, Position.bottomRight([0, 1]), DestroyOnHide);
overlay.domParent = placementEl.find('.global-nav-overlays-container')[0];
overlay.show();
// For tracking clicks to submenu links, we add an attribute to the link being hovered over so we can retrieve
// the tracking prefix from the link's tracking-label attribute.
linkEl.attr('data-active-menu-trigger', true);
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_tab').addClass('hovering');
overlay.on('hide', function() {
// Remove attribute used for tracking
linkEl.removeAttr('data-active-menu-trigger');
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_tab').removeClass('hovering');
});
oldOverlay = overlay;
});
});

var reqs = ['trjs!overlays/Overlay',
'trjs!overlays/styles/flyout',
'trjs!overlays/options/closeOnMouseAway',
'trjs!overlays/position',
'trjs!overlays/options/destroyOnHide'

if (oldOverlay) {
if (oldOverlay.sourceElement == this){
oldOverlay.isOpen() ? oldOverlay.hide('close') : oldOverlay.show();
return; // don't re-open the same overlay.
}
else {
oldOverlay.hide('new-overlay');
}
}
// Create a new overlay
menuEl = menuEl.clone();
var reqs = ['trjs!overlays/Overlay',
'trjs!overlays/styles/flyout',
'trjs!overlays/options/closeOnDocClick',
'trjs!overlays/position',
'trjs!overlays/options/autoReposition'
];
require(reqs, function(Overlay, Flyout, CloseOnDocClick, Position, AutoReposition) {
var overlay = new Overlay(elm[0], new Flyout(menuEl[0], 'global-nav-flyout global-nav-utility'), CloseOnDocClick, Position.bottomLeft([-20, -3]), AutoReposition);
overlay.domParent = placementEl.find('.global-nav-overlays-container')[0];
overlay.show();
elm.addClass('menu-open');
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_icon').addClass('hovering');
overlay.on('hide', function() {
elm.removeClass('menu-open');
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_icon').removeClass('hovering');
});
oldOverlay = overlay;
});
});

placementEl.on('click', '.global-nav-logo', function() {
require(['trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record'], function(taRecord) {
taRecord.setEvtCookie('TopNav', 'click', 'TAlogo', 0, '/Home');
});
});
// Mobile Web Global Nav Persistent Icons
function checkForPersistentIcons() {
var showLogo = $('.first-view', placementEl);
var hideLogo = $('.second-view', placementEl);
var offsetPosition = $(window).scrollTop();
var persistentIcons = $('.persistent-icons', placementEl);
var navIcons = $('.global-nav-icons', persistentIcons);
if (navIcons.length) {
var logo = $('.global-nav-logo');
var pill = $('[data-placement-name="global_nav_geopill"]');
// A - Sideways default state: Logo and icons together, geo pill on second line
// B - Sideways 1st scroll (down): Icons animate to geo pill, logo scrolls out of view
// C - Sideways 2nd scroll (down): Icons locked to geo pill, all elements scroll out of view
//
// A - Internal default state: No logo, geo pill and icons on first line
// B - Internal 1st scroll (down): Icons locked to geo pill, all elements scroll out of view
//
// Adjust icons to placements: Logo then Geopill when available
if (pill.is(':visible')) {
if (offsetPosition < 0) {
navIcons.css({
'top': 0
});
}
else if (offsetPosition >= 0 && offsetPosition <= persistentIcons.height() - pill.height()) {
navIcons.css({
'top': offsetPosition
});
}
}
}
}
// Auto scroll to desired position based on traffic type
function positionSecondView() {
var showLogo = $('.first-view', placementEl);
var hideLogo = $('.second-view', placementEl);
var offsetPosition = $(window).scrollTop();
var persistentIcons = $('.persistent-icons', placementEl);
var navIcons = $('.global-nav-icons', persistentIcons);
if (navIcons.length) {
var logo = $('.global-nav-logo');
var pill = $('[data-placement-name="global_nav_geopill"]');
if (hideLogo.length && pill.is(':visible')) {
offsetPosition = persistentIcons.height() - logo.height();
window.scroll(0, offsetPosition);
navIcons.css({
'position': 'absolute',
'top': 'auto',
'bottom': 0
});
}
}
}
// Global Nav Persistent Single-line Header
function checkForPersistentGlobalNav() {
var persistentGlobalNav = $('.global-nav-persistent', placementEl);
if (persistentGlobalNav.length) {
persistentGlobalNav.toggleClass('fixed', $(window).scrollTop() > placementEl.offset().top);
}
}
require(['trjs!ta/Core/TA.Event'], function(taEvent) {
taEvent.queueForLoad( function() {
positionSecondView();
});
});
window.onscroll = function() {
require(['trjs!utils/throttle'], function(throttle) {
throttle(checkForPersistentIcons(), 0);
throttle(checkForPersistentGlobalNav(), 100);
});
};
return {
checkForPersistentIcons: checkForPersistentIcons,
checkForPersistentGlobalNav: checkForPersistentGlobalNav
};
});

define('Logging', ['vanillajs'], function(vanilla) {
var DEBUG_LEVEL = typeof IS_DEBUG !== 'undefined' && IS_DEBUG ? 3 : -1;
var result = {};
var levels = ['error', 'warn', 'dir', 'info', 'debug'];
for (var i=0; i<levels.length; i++) {
var level = levels[i];
result[level] = (function(level, idx) {
return function() {
if (DEBUG_LEVEL < idx) {
return;
}
if (typeof console === 'undefined' || !console[level] || !console[level].apply) {
return;
}
console[level].apply(console, arguments);
}
})(level, i);
}
result.setLevel = function(newLevel) {
DEBUG_LEVEL = newLevel;
};
return result;
});
define('common/DustRenderer', ['Logging'], function(Logging) {
return function(template, data) {
var dustGlobal = {};
if (require.defined('page-model')) {
dustGlobal = require('page-model').DUST_GLOBAL;
} else {
dustGlobal = DUST_GLOBAL;
}
if (!template || !dust.cache[dustGlobal.LOCALE + template]) {
throw new Error('Template is missing for ' + template);
}
var start = new Date().getTime();
var blob = dust.makeBase(dustGlobal).push(data);
var output = '';
dust.render(dustGlobal.LOCALE + template, blob, function (err, out) {
if (err) {
throw err;
}
output = out;
});
var totalTime = (new Date().getTime() - start);
if (totalTime > 5) {
Logging.warn('Template ' + template + ' took ' + totalTime + 'ms to render');
}
return output;
};
});
define('overlays/styles/flyout', ['vanillajs', 'api-mod'], function(vanilla, api) {
'use strict';
function buildDOM(classes) {
this.container = api.createElement('div', {
'class': 'ui_overlay ui_flyout' + (classes ? ' ' + classes : '')
});
this.contentElement = this.container;
}
var Overlay = function(content, classes) {
return function() {
buildDOM.call(this, classes || this.sourceElement.getAttribute('data-flyout') || '');
this.updateContent(content);
};
};
return Overlay;
});
define('overlays/options/destroyOnHide', ['vanillajs'], function(vanilla){
return function() {
this.hide = function(hideTrigger) {
if (!this.container.overlay) {
return;
}
delete this.container.overlay;
this.domParent.removeChild( this.container );
this.emit('hide', { trigger: hideTrigger });
this.emit('destroy', { trigger: hideTrigger });
this.sourceElement = null;
this.contentElement = null;
return this;
};
};
});
define('overlays/options/fade', ['lib/jquery-amd'], function($){
'use strict';
var NOOP = function(){};
var fadeInClass = 'fade_in';
var fadeOutClass = 'fade_out';
function addClass(cl){
$(this.container).addClass(cl);
$(this.shade).addClass(cl);
}
function removeClass(cl){
$(this.container).removeClass(cl);
$(this.shade).removeClass(cl);
}
var BOTH = [
function(fadeType){
addClass.call(this, fadeType.cl);
},
function(fadeType){
addClass.call(this, fadeInClass);
},
NOOP,
function(fadeType){
removeClass.call(this, fadeInClass);
},
NOOP
];
var ONLY_IN = [
NOOP,
function(fadeType){
addClass.call(this, fadeType.cl);
addClass.call(this, fadeInClass);
},
function(fadeType){
removeClass.call(this, fadeType.cl);
removeClass.call(this, fadeInClass);
},
NOOP,
NOOP
];
var ONLY_OUT = [
NOOP,
NOOP,
NOOP,
function(fadeType){
addClass.call(this, fadeType.out);
addClass.call(this, fadeOutClass);
},
function(fadeType){
removeClass.call(this, fadeType.out);
removeClass.call(this, fadeOutClass);
}
];
var Fade = function(fadeType, onShow, onHide){
return function() {
if (!fadeType) { return; }
onShow = onShow !== false;
onHide = onHide !== false;
var oldShow = this.show;
var oldHide = this.hide;
var fns = onShow && onHide ? BOTH : onShow ? ONLY_IN : ONLY_OUT;
fns[0].call(this, fadeType);
onShow && (this.show = function() {
var args = arguments;
oldShow && oldShow.apply(this, args);
fns[1].call(this, fadeType);
setTimeout(function(){
fns[2].call(this, fadeType);
}.bind(this), fadeType.len);
}.bind(this));
onHide && (this.hide = function() {
var args = arguments;
fns[3].call(this, fadeType);
setTimeout(function() {
fns[4].call(this, fadeType);
oldHide && oldHide.apply(this, args);
}.bind(this), fadeType.len);
}.bind(this));
};
};
Fade.NONE = {cl: 'fade_none', out: 'fade_out_none', len: 0};
Fade.SHORT = {cl: 'fade_short', out: 'fade_out_short', len: 250};
Fade.NORMAL = {cl: 'fade_normal', out: 'fade_out_normal', len: 500};
Fade.LONG = {cl: 'fade_long', out: 'fade_out_long', len: 1000};
return Fade;
});
require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {

return (new Date().getTime() - time) < (2 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
};
var _isTimeWithin30Days = function(time) {
return (new Date().getTime() - time) < (30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
};

var _showTest1IfNeeded = function(isInControl, storageKey) {

}
});
};

Storage.set(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY, true);

_displayOverlay($testEl);
}
Storage.set(storageKey, true);
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(storageKey, "flyout_shown", servletName + "|recents_" + response.data.length, 0, false);
}
});
};

if (servletName === 'Hotel_Review') {
return;

_getRecentLocations(function(response) {
if (response.data && response.data.length >= 2 && !_isTimeWithin2Hours(response.data[1].date)) {
var openMyTripsIfNeeded = function(isInControl, storageKey) {
if (_isOverlayOnPage()) {
Storage.set(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY, true);
return;
}
Storage.set(storageKey, true);

radio.trigger('run-my-trips-test-3');
} else {
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(storageKey, "flyout_shown", servletName + "|recents_" + response.data.length, 0, false);
}
};
if (require('page-model').session.user_id) {
_getTripLists(function(response) {
if (!response.data || response.data.length == 0) {
openMyTripsIfNeeded(isInControl, storageKey);
}
});
} else {
openMyTripsIfNeeded(isInControl, storageKey);
}
}
});
};
var _showTestFlyout = function() {

if (Storage.has(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY)) {
return;
}
if ($root.find('.test-container')) {
var isTAReferrer = $root.find('.test-container').attr('data-is-ta-referrer');
}
if ($testEl.length) {
var testVersion = $testEl.attr('data-test-version');
var storageKey = STORAGE_TEST_KEY_PREFIX + testVersion;
// Attempt to show the test flyout base on test version
if (testVersion == '1' && !Storage.has(storageKey)) {
_showTest1IfNeeded(false, storageKey);
} else if (testVersion == '2' && !isTAReferrer && !Storage.has(storageKey)) {
_showTest2IfNeeded(false, storageKey);
} else if (testVersion == '3' && !isTAReferrer && !Storage.has(storageKey)) {
_showTest3IfNeeded(false, storageKey);
}
} else if ($controlEl.length) {
// The user could have seen overlay if he/she in test group
if (!Storage.has(STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '1')) {
_showTest1IfNeeded(true, STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '1');
}
if (!Storage.has(STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '2') && !isTAReferrer) {
_showTest2IfNeeded(true, STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '2');
}
if (!Storage.has(STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '3') && !isTAReferrer) {
_showTest3IfNeeded(true, STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '3');
}
}
}, 800);
};

&& $quickSaveEl.length > 0
&& Storage.has(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY)
&& !Storage.get(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY)
&& api.scrollTop() == 0) {

Storage.set(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY, true);
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY, "flyout_shown", servletName, 0, false);
}
}, 1000);
};

}

define([
'placement',
'lib/jquery-amd'
], function(
placement,
$
) {
'use strict';
var placementEl = $('#' + placement.id);
var globalNavMenus = $('[data-placement-name="global_nav_menus"]');
// Tracking: Catch-all
var _trackNavClick = function(elmt, category) {
var trackingLabel = $(elmt).data('trackingLabel');
// Handle links to /# (Help Center) or links opening new window
require(['trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record'], function(taRecord) {
if(/\/#\s*$/.test(elmt.href) || elmt.target == '_blank') {
taRecord.trackEventOnPage(category, 'click', trackingLabel);
} else {
taRecord.setEvtCookie(category, 'click', trackingLabel, 0, elmt.href);
}
});
};
// Tracking: Catches all of the non-submenu links that require tracking
// Links only qualify if they have the data-tracking-label attribute.
globalNavMenus.on('click', 'a.global-nav-link[data-tracking-label]', function() {
_trackNavClick(this, 'TopNav');
});
// Tracking for links in submenus works by looking up the active-menu-trigger
// (link that triggered the dropdown) and using it's tracking-label as a prefix
globalNavMenus.on('click', 'a.subLink', function() {
var triggerEl = $("[data-active-menu-trigger][data-tracking-label]", placementEl);
var trackingLabel = triggerEl.data('trackingLabel') + "_sublink";
_trackNavClick(this, 'TopNav');
});
});

define('cpm/DblClickAPI', ['lib/jquery-amd', 'ta/Core/TA.Store', 'ta/util/Error'],
function( $, taStore, taError) {
'use strict';
window.googletag = window.googletag || {};
googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];
var exports = {};
var _initialized = false;
var _enableSingleRequestMode = false;
function _roundedWinSize() {
var rawW = $(window).width();
var rawH = $(window).height();
var scale = 100;
var w = Math.floor(rawW/scale)*scale;
var h = Math.floor(rawH/scale)*scale;
w = (w > 2000) ? 9999 : w;
h = (h > 1500) ? 9999 : h;
return 'w' + w + '_h' + h;
}
function _addPageTargeting(bIsMobileWeb) {
try {
var targeting = taStore.retrieve('ads.pageTargeting') || {};
if(!bIsMobileWeb) {
targeting.win_size = _roundedWinSize();
}
for( var key in targeting ) {
googletag.pubads().setTargeting(key, targeting[key]);
}
} catch(e) {
taError.record(e, 'DblClickAPI init: unable to add page targeting');
}
}
function _addPpid() {
var ppid = taStore.retrieve('ads.ppid');
if (ppid) {
googletag.pubads().setPublisherProvidedId(ppid);
}
}
exports.enableSingleRequestMode = function() {
_enableSingleRequestMode = true;
};
exports.init = function(bIsMobileWeb, onAdRenderHandler) {
if(_initialized) {
return;
}
_initialized = true;
var gads=document.createElement('script');
gads.async=true;
gads.type='text/javascript';
gads.src='//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';
var node=document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
node.parentNode.insertBefore(gads,node);
googletag.cmd.push(function(){
_addPpid();
_addPageTargeting(bIsMobileWeb);
if(taStore.has('jwplayerHelper.adUrl')) {
googletag.pubads().enableVideoAds();
}
googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', onAdRenderHandler);
if(_enableSingleRequestMode) {
googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
}
googletag.enableServices();
});
};
return exports;
});
define('cpm/AdController', ['lib/jquery-amd', 'utils/throttle', 'ta/util/Error'],
function( $, throttle, taError) {
'use strict';
var exports = {};
var _deferAdsScrollHandler = throttle(_handleScroll, 150);
var _scrollHandlerRunning = false;
var _deferredAds = [];
var _injectionPaused = false;
var _injectOnScrollUpReady = true;
function _deferAd(tripAd) {
var bQueued = false;
if(_deferredAds.length) {
for(var i=0; i < _deferredAds.length; i++ ) {
var deferredAd = _deferredAds[i];
if(deferredAd.adId == tripAd.adId) {
bQueued = true;
break;
}
}
if(!bQueued) {
_deferredAds.push(tripAd);
}
} else {
_deferredAds.push(tripAd);
if(!_scrollHandlerRunning) {
_scrollHandlerRunning = true;
$(window).on('scroll', _deferAdsScrollHandler);
}
}
}
function _handleScroll() {
try {
var bAdInjected = false;
for(var i = 0, len=_deferredAds.length; i < len; i++) {
var tgtAd = _deferredAds[i];
if(tgtAd && tgtAd.isVisible() && tgtAd.isInView()) {
tgtAd.inject();
bAdInjected = true;
delete _deferredAds[i];
}
}
if(bAdInjected) {
var remainingAds = [];
_deferredAds.forEach(function(ad) {
if(typeof ad != "undefined") {
remainingAds.push(ad);
}
});
_deferredAds = remainingAds;
}
if(_deferredAds.length == 0) {
_scrollHandlerRunning = false;
$(window).off('scroll', _deferAdsScrollHandler);
}
} catch (e) {
_scrollHandlerRunning = false;
$(window).off('scroll', _deferAdsScrollHandler);
var elemId = ( tgtAd && tgtAd.id ) ? tgtAd.id : 'undefined';
var sMsg = 'deferAds: Error with defer. ad ID: ' + elemId;
taError.record(e, sMsg);
}
}
exports.deferAd = _deferAd;
exports.setInjectionPaused = function(bPause) {
_injectionPaused = bPause;
};
exports.injectionPaused = function() {
return _injectionPaused;
};
exports.setInjectOnScrollUpReady = function(bReady) {
_injectOnScrollUpReady = bReady;
};
exports.injectOnScrollUpReady = function() {
return _injectOnScrollUpReady;
};
return exports;
});
define('cpm/TripAd', ['lib/jquery-amd', 'ns-exporter', 'cpm/AdController', 'ta/Core/TA.Store', 'ta/util/Error'],
function( $, nsExporter, adController, taStore, taError) {
'use strict';
var exports = {};
var __getTabletOrientation = function() {
return (window.screen && window.screen.orientation) ? window.screen.orientation.type : null;
};
var __cloneTripAdForRefresh = function(adStub, slotTargeting, options) {
if(!(adStub && adStub.tgt)) {
return;
}
try {
var updatedTgtId = __buildRefreshAdId(adStub);
if(!updatedTgtId) {
throw new Error('unable to build refresh ad id for ' + adStub.tgt);
}
var adElem = document.getElementById(adStub.tgt);
var newAd = adElem.cloneNode(false);
newAd.id = updatedTgtId;
$(newAd).removeClass('taEmpty');
if(!$(newAd).hasClass('gutterad')) {
$(newAd).attr('style','');
}
var adParent = adElem.parentNode;
adParent.replaceChild(newAd, adElem);
adStub.tgt = updatedTgtId;
var clonedTripAd = exports.init(adStub, options);
clonedTripAd.addTargeting(slotTargeting);
clonedTripAd.injectWhenViewable();
} catch(e) {
taError.record(e, 'error cloning ad for refresh');
}
};
var __buildRefreshAdId = function(adStub) {
var refreshId;
try {
var id = adStub.tgt;
if(id.match(/ref\d+/)) {
var num = parseInt(id.match(/ref(\d+)/)[1], 10) + 1;
refreshId = id.replace(/ref\d+/, 'ref' + num);
} else {
refreshId = id + '-ref1';
}
} catch(e) {
taError.record(e, 'error building refresh ad id');
}
return refreshId;
};
exports.init = function(adStub, options) {
if(!document.getElementById(adStub.tgt)) {
return null;
}
var TripAd = (function(adStub, options){
var _options = {
collapse: true
};
_options = $.extend(_options, options);
var _adStub = adStub;
var _adBase = adStub.base;
var _adSizes = adStub.size;
var _adId = adStub.tgt;
var _adElem = document.getElementById(_adId);
var _adSlot;
var _slotTargeting = {};
var _adInjected = false;
var _refreshWithNewContext = true;
var _hasLoggedError = false;
var _injectOnScrollUp = false;
var _reservedHeight = $(_adElem).parent('.ad').height() || 0;
var _addSlotTargeting = function(targetingJSON) {
try {
targetingJSON = _mergeTargeting(targetingJSON);
if(targetingJSON.pos) {
targetingJSON.pos = _updatePositionValue(targetingJSON.pos);
}
var orientation = __getTabletOrientation();
if(window.isTabletOnFullSite && orientation) {
targetingJSON.oriented = /portrait/.test(orientation) ? 'p' : 'l';
}
_slotTargeting = targetingJSON;
for( var key in targetingJSON ) {
_adSlot.setTargeting( key, targetingJSON[key] );
}
} catch(e) {
taError.record(e, 'error applying ad slot targeting');
}
};
var _addElementTargeting = function() {
if( _adElem && _adElem.getAttribute('data-targeting') ) {
var targeting = _adElem.getAttribute('data-targeting');
if( window.JSON && JSON.parse ) {
try {
var targetingJSON = JSON.parse(targeting.replace(/'/g,"\""));
_addSlotTargeting(targetingJSON);
} catch(e) {
taError.record(e, 'error applying element ad targeting');
}
}
}
};
var _updatePositionValue = function(originalVal) {
var updatedVals = [];
var additionalVals = { 'top':'a', 'bottom':'b' };
if(Array.isArray(originalVal)) {
originalVal.forEach( function(val){
if( additionalVals[val] ) {
updatedVals.push(val);
updatedVals.push(additionalVals[val]);
}
});
} else {
if( additionalVals[originalVal] ) {
updatedVals.push(originalVal);
updatedVals.push(additionalVals[originalVal]);
}
}
return (updatedVals.length) ? updatedVals : originalVal;
};
var _mergeTargeting = function(newJSON) {
var targeting = _slotTargeting;
for(var key in newJSON) {
if(targeting[key] == newJSON[key]) {
continue;
}
if(key == 'kw' || key == 'proptype') {
targeting[key] = newJSON[key];
continue;
}
if(!targeting[key]) {
targeting[key] = newJSON[key];
} else {
if(!Array.isArray(targeting[key])){
targeting[key] = [targeting[key]];
}
if(!Array.isArray(newJSON[key])) {
newJSON[key] = [newJSON[key]];
}
var allVals = targeting[key].concat(newJSON[key]);
var newVals = [];
for(var i=allVals.length - 1; i > -1; i--) {
var nextVal = allVals.pop();
if($.inArray(nextVal, newVals) === -1){
newVals.push(nextVal);
}
}
targeting[key] = newVals.reverse();
}
}
return targeting;
};
var _inject = function(bNewContext) {
if(bNewContext == false) {
_refreshWithNewContext = false;
}
try {
var adElem = document.getElementById(_adStub.tgt);
if ($(adElem).parent('.ad').add(adElem).hasClass('inactive')) {
return;
}
if(_adInjected) {
if(adElem) {
_adStub.isExpanded = !$(adElem).hasClass('taEmpty') && $(adElem).is(':visible');
$(adElem).removeClass('taEmpty');
if(_refreshWithNewContext) {
googletag.pubads().refresh([_adSlot]);
} else {
_refresh();
}
} else {
throw new Error('ad refresh fail, elem does not exist: ' + _adId);
}
} else {
googletag.display(_adId);
_adInjected = true;
}
} catch(e) {
if(!_hasLoggedError) {
taError.record(e, 'unable to inject TripAd for target: ' + _adId);
_hasLoggedError = true;
}
}
};
var _defer = function() {
var tripAd = taStore.retrieve('tripads.'+ _adId);
if (tripAd) {
adController.deferAd(tripAd);
}
};
var _refresh = function() {
__cloneTripAdForRefresh(_adStub, _slotTargeting, _options);
};
var _getSelector = function(adElem) {
if (adElem && adElem.id) {
return '#' + adElem.id;
} else {
return '';
}
};
var _getPosY = function() {
return $(_getSelector(_adElem)).offset().top;
};
var _isInView = function() {
if(adController.injectionPaused()) {
return false;
}
var scrollY = $(window).scrollTop();
if(_injectOnScrollUp) {
return adController.injectOnScrollUpReady() && _getPosY() + _reservedHeight > scrollY;
} else {
return _getPosY() < scrollY + $(window).height();
}
};
var _checkForScrollUpInjection = function(){
var scrollY = $(window).scrollTop();
_injectOnScrollUp = adController.injectOnScrollUpReady() && scrollY > _getPosY() + _reservedHeight;
};
try {
if ((adStub.tgt.indexOf('4x4') == -1) && (adStub.tgt.indexOf('1x1') == -1)) {
_adSizes.push('fluid');
}
if(!taStore.has('tripads.' + _adId)) {
_adSlot = googletag.defineSlot(_adBase,_adSizes,_adId)
.addService(googletag.pubads())
.setCollapseEmptyDiv(_options.collapse, !_adStub.isExpanded);
if(adStub.custom_targeting && adStub.custom_targeting['companion']) {
_adSlot.addService(googletag.companionAds());
}
} else {
throw new Error('ad slot has already been created');
}
if(adStub.custom_targeting) {
_addSlotTargeting(adStub.custom_targeting);
}
_addElementTargeting();
} catch(e) {
taError.record('Unable to create TripAd for target ' + _adId + ': ' + e.message);
return null;
}
return {
adId: _adId,
slotTargeting: _slotTargeting,
addTargeting: function(targetingJSON) {
_addSlotTargeting(targetingJSON);
},
inject: _inject,
refresh: _refresh,
injectWhenViewable: function(bNewContext) {
if(bNewContext == false) {
_refreshWithNewContext = false;
}
try {
_checkForScrollUpInjection();
if(_isInView()) {
_inject(_refreshWithNewContext);
} else {
_defer();
}
} catch(e) {
taError.record(e, 'unable to inject/defer TripAd');
}
},
defer: _defer,
isInView: _isInView,
checkForScrollUpInjection: _checkForScrollUpInjection,
isVisible: function() {
if(_adElem) {
return $(_getSelector(_adElem)).is(':visible') && $(_getSelector(_adElem)).css('visibility')!='hidden';
}
return false;
}
};
})(adStub, options);
if(TripAd && TripAd.adId) {
taStore.store('tripads.'+ TripAd.adId, TripAd);
}
return TripAd;
};
return exports;
});
require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'enable_cpm_content','handlers',['handlers']);
/*****
*  The AMD version of ta/common/behavior/Ads.js as a placement.
*
*  @exports disableRefresh - used by the ad debugger primarily
*  @exports collapseAd - used by the "inventory pixel" collapsers
*
*  This placement currently supports:
*
*  Initializing the DoubleClick API
*  Injection of ads availablein-view at pageload
*  Handling pageload ads
*  Deferred scroll-into-view injection
*  Collapsing the inventory pixel ad
*  Inject on scroll-up for urls with mid-page anchor targets
*  Subscribing to various refresh events (tab focus, filters etc.)
*  Injection pausing during auto scroll
*  Injection of ads post page-load via "queueForInjection"
*  The automatic 2x1 "Attribution pixel" injection
*
*  For ajax-related ads, they can be injected via queueForInjection:
*  ta.common.ads.queueForInjection([elemId, elemId])
*
*  Refreshing all the ads on the page is handled by adding an observer and firing an event when the refresh should happen:
*  taEvent.on('onHACUpdateComplete',  _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
*
*  Future updates will incorporate:
*
*  1) Hotel-type filtering updates: updateHotelStyle updateHotelType
*  2) Gutter-ad related methods
*  3) Video preroll
*  4) Implementation of methods to inject ads in ajax responses ( HAC response etc. )
*
*****/
/* globals googletag, define */
define(['placement', 'lib/jquery-amd', 'cpm/DblClickAPI', 'cpm/AdController', 'cpm/TripAd', 'ns-exporter', 'utils/throttle', 'ta/Core/TA.Event', 'ta/Core/TA.Store', 'ta/Core/TA.Record', 'ta/util/Error'],
function( placement, $, dblClick, adController, adSlot, nsExporter, throttle, taEvent, taStore, taRecord, taError) {
'use strict';
var _initialized = false;
var _exports = {};
// used by injectOnScrollUp ads, mostly when url target is #REVIEWS etc.
var _scrollOnPageLoad = 0;
// for "refreshAllAds" refreshes
var _lastRefreshAll = new Date().getTime();
var _minRefreshAllMS = 10000;
// for disabling event/filter ad refreshes
var _enableRefresh = true;
// check for "attribution" tests (hidden 2x1 ad call)
var _checkForAttributionPixel = true;
//check for "attribution" tests (hidden 2x1 ad call) in photo gallery
var _checkForPhotoGalleryAttributionPixel = true;
// Attribution pixel for the main page
var _mainPageAttrPixel = 'gpt-ad-2x1';
// Attribution pixel for the photo light box
var _photoLightBoxAttrPixel = 'gpt-ad-2x1-b';
// URL hash segment for photo album viewer
var _LEGACY_PHOTO_FRAGMENT = '#photos';
/**
* Subscribe to various events that trigger ad refreshes
*
* @private
*/
function _subscribeToEvents() {
// listen for ad hoc ad injection requests
taEvent.on('ads.queueForInjection', _queueForInjection);
// tablet orientation-change
if (window.isTabletOnFullSite) {
$(window).on('orientationchange', _orientationChange);
}
// if not in control for event refresh tests
if(!taStore.has('ads.disableEventRefresh')) {
// refresh on tab focus with 10 second minimum between refreshes
$(window).on('focus', function() { _refreshAllAdsPolitely(true); });
// closing modal overlays etc.
taEvent.on('onOverlayClose', _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
// TODO: Do we really want to refresh on calendar display? ( bad UX )
}
// TODO (Restaurants): refactor to use standard patterns
// taEvent.on('onRestaurantFilterChange',
// TODO (Hotels): refactor to use standard patterns
// taEvent.on('onUpdateHACAds', ta.common.ads.updateHotelHacAds);
if(window.pageServlet === 'Hotels') {
taEvent.on('adSizeChanged', _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
// TODO: still using window.fireEvent
} else if(window.pageServlet === 'Attractions') {
taEvent.on('onAttractionFilterChange', _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
} else if(window.pageServlet === 'SmartDeals') {
// This is the only ad on the page, setting isNewContext:true (no need to preserve pageload context)
ta.on('onSmartDealsUpdateComplete', function(){ _queueForInjection({'elemIds':['gpt-ad-728x90-a'],'isNewContext':true }); });
} else if(window.pageServlet === 'Restaurant_Review') {
taEvent.on('review_filters.filter_changed', _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
taEvent.on('review_keyword_search.tag_toggled', _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
} else if((window.pageServlet === 'HotelsList' && taStore.retrieve('ta.p13n.blender_with_category_xsells.enabled')) ||
window.pageServlet === 'ThemePark') {
taEvent.on('onHACUpdateComplete',  _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
} else if(window.pageServlet === 'VRACSearch' && taStore.retrieve('vrDblClickAdCallsEnabled')) {
taEvent.on('onVRACSearchFilterChange', _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
} else if(window.pageServlet === 'Tourism') {
taEvent.on('scrollingTabs_Start', _pauseOnScrollInjection );
taEvent.on('scrollingTabs_End', _resumeOnScrollInjection );
// TODO: ADS-2513 - new event added, the gutter ad will be refreshed when user expand the IB room list
// ta.on('tabExpand_Start', ta.common.ads.roomListExpandStart );
// ta.on('tabExpand_End', ta.common.ads.refreshWhenRoomListExpand );
// Review pages
} else if(window.pageServlet === 'Hotel_Review' ||
window.pageServlet === 'Attraction_Review' ||
window.pageServlet === 'Restaurant_Review') {
taEvent.on('scrollingTabs_Start', _pauseOnScrollInjection );
taEvent.on('scrollingTabs_End', _resumeOnScrollInjection );
// TODO: ADS-2513 - new event added, the gutter ad will be refreshed when user expand the IB room list
// ta.on('tabExpand_Start', ta.common.ads.roomListExpandStart );
// ta.on('tabExpand_End', ta.common.ads.refreshWhenRoomListExpand );
// TODO: still using window.fireEvent
taEvent.on('ReviewExpanded', _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
} else if(window.pageServlet === 'Airlines') {
taEvent.on('airlinesPlacementLoad', _refreshAllAdsPolitely);
}
}
/**
* Refresh ads on tablet orientation change
*
* @private
*/
function _orientationChange() {
_refreshAllAdsPolitely(true);
}
/**
* Renders a hidden 2x1 Ad Call just below the first rendered ad on the page
* Controlled by the cpm_attribution_pixel feature
*
* @param {String} domId - of the ad currently being injected
* @param {String} adId - if for the attribution pixel
*
* @private
*/
function _handleAttributionPixel(domId, adId) {
adId = adId || _mainPageAttrPixel;
try {
// check feature gating
if(taStore.retrieve('ads.attributionPixel') !== true) {
_checkForAttributionPixel = false;
_checkForPhotoGalleryAttributionPixel = false;
return;
}
var adElem = $('#' + domId);
// if the "first Ad" is a real ad and not the collapser
if(adElem.is(':visible') && !adElem.hasClass('taEmpty')) {
var ajaxTargeting = {};
// Set the appropriate flag based on the ad container type
if(_mainPageAttrPixel === adId) {
_checkForAttributionPixel = false;
}
else if(_photoLightBoxAttrPixel === adId) {
_checkForPhotoGalleryAttributionPixel = false;
ajaxTargeting = taStore.retrieve('ads.locationphotoalbum.pageTargeting', {});
}
// create and insert the target div
var pixelTgt = $('<div />', { 'id': adId, 'class':'gptAd hidden'});
// insert after first-viewed ad
pixelTgt.insertAfter(adElem);
// build the adStub
var adBase = taStore.retrieve('ads.gptBase');
if(adBase) {
var adStub = {'base':adBase,'size':[[2,1]],'tgt':adId,'custom_targeting':{'disable_event_refresh':true}};
// Create the wrapped Ad
var tripAd = adSlot.init(adStub, {});
if(tripAd) {
if(!$.isEmptyObject(ajaxTargeting)) {
tripAd.addTargeting(ajaxTargeting);
}
tripAd.inject();
// For AdDebug visibility, store the ad
taStore.store('tripads.' + adId,tripAd);
} else {
throw new Error('TripAd is null');
}
} else {
throw new Error('adBase not found');
}
}
} catch(err) {
taError.record(err, 'error rendering CPM attribution pixel');
}
}
/**
* Things to handle anytime an ad is injected
*
* @param {Event} event - the DoubleClick-fired "slotRenderEnded" event
*
* @private
*/
function _postRenderAdProcessing(event) {
var slotId = event && event.slot && event.slot.getSlotId && event.slot.getSlotId();
var domId = slotId && slotId.getDomId ? slotId.getDomId() : null;
var creativeId = event && event.creativeId;
var advertiserId = event && event.advertiserId;
// Attribution pixel tests: fire with first rendered ad on main page, or on the location photo album page
var isPhotoAlbum = window.location.hash.indexOf(_LEGACY_PHOTO_FRAGMENT) >= 0;
if(_checkForPhotoGalleryAttributionPixel && isPhotoAlbum) {
_handleAttributionPixel(domId, _photoLightBoxAttrPixel);
} else if(_checkForAttributionPixel && !isPhotoAlbum) {
_handleAttributionPixel(domId, _mainPageAttrPixel);
}
// Add creative id attribute on slot render
_addCreativeIdOnSlotRender(event);
// fire an event to notify other ads of possible page layout changes etc.
// Currently used by the gutter ad to re-position
taEvent.fireEvent('onAdRender', {'domId': domId, 'advertiserId': advertiserId, 'creativeId': creativeId});
var adElt = $('#' + domId);
if(!adElt.hasClass('taEmpty')) {
adElt.parent('.ad').addClass('loaded');
}
}
/**
* Adds the data-creative-id attribute to the ad wrapper when the ad renders
*
* @paraqm {Event} event - the DoubleClick-fired "slotRenderEnded" event
*
* @private
*/
function _addCreativeIdOnSlotRender(event) {
try {
// if a non-empty ad is returned
if(event && event.slot && event.creativeId) {
var adWrapper = $('#' + event.slot.getSlotId().getDomId());
adWrapper.attr('data-creative-id', event.creativeId);
adWrapper.attr('data-advertiser-id', event.advertiserId);
}
} catch(e) {
// creative id is used to debug ads, no need to log errors
}
}
/**
* Pause onScroll ad injection (during autoScroll etc.)
*
* @private
*/
function _pauseOnScrollInjection() {
adController.setInjectionPaused(true);
// TODO: gutterAd snippet
}
/**
* Resume onScroll ad injection (after autoScroll etc.)
*
* @private
*/
function _resumeOnScrollInjection() {
adController.setInjectionPaused(false);
// TODO: gutterAd snippet
}
/**
* Listens for first scroll on pages with link targets (#REVIEWS)
*
* @private
*/
function _enableScrollUpInjection() {
adController.setInjectOnScrollUpReady(true);
$(window).off('scroll', _enableScrollUpInjection);
}
/**
* For use by initDoubleClick on page load.
* If the url includes an anchor ( like #REVIEWS ) then determine
* the initial scroll position so we don't inject ads
* (i.e. leaderboard) that will not be seen on page load.
*
* @param limitFrequency - true to prevent exessive ad refreshes during filtering etc.
*
* @returns {Number} - the expected onload page scroll
*
* @private
*/
function _getPageLoadScroll() {
var expectedScrollY = 0;
if(window.location.hash) {
var anchor = document.getElementById(window.location.hash);
if(anchor) {
// Testing "visible" is expensive, so testing offset().top > 0 ( display:none elements return 0 )
var anchorTop = $(anchor).offset().top;
if(anchorTop > 0) {
// ScrollingTabs will alter the scroll target so check for stored value
if(taStore.has('scrollingTabs.scrollOnPageLoad')) {
expectedScrollY = taStore.retrieve('scrollingTabs.scrollOnPageLoad');
} else {
expectedScrollY = anchorTop;
}
/**
* ADS-839: If there's a down-page target, make sure we've at least started scrolling to the anchor (#REVIEWS)
*
* IE will report initial scroll values of 0, etc. on pageload
* prior to scrolling to the url hash/anchor (i.e. #REVIEWS)
* We need to ignore these initial values and wait until
* the page has scrolled to the anchor, before enabling ad injection onScrollUp
*/
if(expectedScrollY > 0) {
var curScrollY = $(window).scrollTop();
// page is slow, hasn't scrolled to target yet
if(curScrollY == 0) {
adController.setInjectOnScrollUpReady(false);
// This runs on first scroll only
$(window).on('scroll', _enableScrollUpInjection);
}
}
}
}
}
return expectedScrollY;
}
/**
* Handles refresh specifics for a single TripAd object when refreshing the ads on the page
*
* @param {Boolean} limitFrequency - true to prevent exessive ad refreshes during filtering etc.
*
* @private
*/
function _okToRefreshAll(limitFrequency) {
// check that refreshes haven't been disabled ( i.e. by an expandable creative )
if(!_enableRefresh) {
return false;
}
if (!limitFrequency) {
return true;
}
var now = new Date().getTime();
if(now - _lastRefreshAll > _minRefreshAllMS) {
_lastRefreshAll = now;
return true;
} else {
return false;
}
}
/**
* Handles refresh specifics for a single TripAd object when refreshing the ads on the page
*
* @param {Object} adTgt - the related ad dom element
* @param {Object} tripad - the ad object
*
* @returns {Boolean}
*
* @private
*/
function _adIsRefreshable(adTgt, tripad) {
var refreshable = false;
if(adTgt) {
refreshable = true;
// check for disabled ads (due to modals, window resize, etc.)
if($(adTgt).parent('.ad.inactive').length) {
return false;
}
// no need to refresh map sponsor ads, except those in hac responses
if(tripad && tripad.slotTargeting && tripad.slotTargeting.disable_event_refresh) {
return false;
}
// TODO check/reset gutter ad
}
return refreshable;
}
/**
* Handles refresh specifics for a single TripAd object when refreshing the ads on the page
*
* @param {Object} tripad - the ad object
*
* @private
*/
function _handleAdRefresh(tripad) {
if(tripad) {
// TODO: scrolling ad check/reset
// flag ads for inject on scroll up/down
var wrappedElem = $(tripad.adElem);
if (wrappedElem.length) {
tripad.injectWhenViewable(false);
}
}
}
/**
* Push the ad refresh to the back of the Queue to allow other things to run first
*
* @param {Boolean} limitFrequency - true to prevent excessive refreshing during filtering etc.
*
* @private
*/
function _refreshAllAdsPolitely(limitFrequency) {
window.setTimeout(function(){ _refreshAllAds(!!limitFrequency); }, 1);
}
/**
* Retrieves all page-load ad stubs and refreshes the ads (defers out-of-view)
*
* @param {Boolean} limitFrequency - true to prevent excessive refreshing during filtering etc.
*
* @private
*/
function _refreshAllAds(limitFrequency) {
// wait at least 10 seconds bewteen refreshes unless explicitly say ignore the time constraint
if(!_okToRefreshAll(limitFrequency)) {
return;
}
// Make sure DoubleClick API is loaded ( ads can be added after pageload )
_checkForAPILoaded();
googletag.cmd.push( function() {
try{
var adStubs = _getAdStubs();
if(adStubs) {
// Set a new correlator (context) when refreshing ads
// And always refresh all (unless you're in a modal photo gallery etc.)
googletag.pubads().updateCorrelator();
for(var i = 0; i < adStubs.length; i++) {
var adStub = adStubs[i];
// Ajax updates may have reverted the -ref1, etc. check for expected and original id
var adTgt = document.getElementById(adStub.tgt) || document.getElementById(adStub.tgt.replace(/-ref\d+/,''));
var tripad = _getAd(adStub);
if(adTgt && tripad) {
if(_adIsRefreshable(adTgt, tripad)) {
_handleAdRefresh(tripad);
}
}
}
}
} catch(e) {
taError.record(e, 'error refreshing all ads');
}
});
}
/**
* Called on pageload to inject visible ads and queue theb rest for onScroll injection
*
* @private
*/
function _injectViewable() {
// determine the initial scroll for the page
_scrollOnPageLoad = _getPageLoadScroll();
// inject viewable ads, store deferred
var ads = _getAdStubs();
if( ads && ads.length ) {
for(var i=0; i < ads.length; i++ ) {
var adStub = ads[i];
if( adStub.tgt ) {
var adElem = document.getElementById(adStub.tgt);
// Note: skip ads marked for manual injection
if(adElem && !$(adElem).hasClass('delayAd')) {
try {
var tripAd = adSlot.init(adStub, {});
if(tripAd) {
// If the page url anchors the user down past the ad (i.e. #REVIEWS),
// we'll flag for scroll UP injection
tripAd.checkForScrollUpInjection();
if(tripAd.isInView()) {
tripAd.inject();
} else {
tripAd.defer();
}
}
} catch(e) {
// We've confirmed that the ad target (adElem) is on the page so
// if we can't create the TripAd from the adStub JSON we should log an error
taError.record(e, 'unable to create TripAd object for ' + adStub.tgt);
}
}
}
}
}
}
/**
* Retrieve the adStub JSON
*
* @param {String} ajaxServlet - servlet name for adStub JSON retrieval
*
* @returns {Array} of adStub Objects
*
* @private
*/
function _getAdStubs(ajaxServlet) {
var adStubs = ajaxServlet ? taStore.retrieve('ads.' + ajaxServlet + '.adStubs') : taStore.retrieve('ads.adStubs');
if(adStubs && adStubs.adTypes) {
// Someone made the stubs a node...
return adStubs.adTypes;
}
return null;
}
/**
* This method returns a reference to a previously created TripAd object,
* or if needed, creates the object.
*
* TripAds can be retrieved via: ta.retrieve('tripads.gpt-ad-728x90-970x66'), etc.
* If the ad has not been created/stored it will be created from the ad stub JSON:
* ta.retrieve('ads.adStubs')
*
* @param {Object} adStub - JSON info for creating ad
* @param {String} ajaxServlet - optional ajax servlet name for retrieveing correct ad Stub
*
* @returns {Object} the TripAd object
*
* @nullable
* @private
*/
function _getAd(adStub, ajaxServlet) {
var tripad = null;
if(adStub) {
try {
// method can be called with stub object or div id
// Object
if(adStub.tgt) {
// first check for stored reference
var storedAd = 'tripads.' + adStub.tgt;
if(taStore.has(storedAd)) {
tripad = taStore.retrieve(storedAd);
// refresh ad elem reference in case the target has been replaced via ajax
var adElem = document.getElementById(tripad.adId);
if(adElem) {
tripad.adElem = adElem;
} else {
// Ajax updates may have reverted the -ref1, etc. check for initial ID
var fallbackElem = document.getElementById(adStub.tgt.replace(/-ref\d+/,''));
if(fallbackElem) {
tripad.adElem = fallbackElem;
tripad.adId = tripad.id = fallbackElem.id;
} else {
tripad = null;
}
}
// return a new TripAd
} else {
try {
tripad = adSlot.init(adStub, {});
} catch(e) {
// fail with null tripad
return null;
}
}
// Id
} else {
// we've been passed an id so let's rename adStub
var reqId = adStub;
var adStubs = _getAdStubs(ajaxServlet);
if(adStubs) {
for(var i=0; i < adStubs.length; i++){
var stub = adStubs[i];
/**
* Ad stubs contain a reference to the current refresh id (-ref1 -ref2 etc.)
* Ad target divs in ajaxed content (HAC!) will have an id that has been reset (no -ref1 etc.)
* Ad injection will fail unless we sync the Ids to the ad stub value.
*/
if(stub.tgt &&
/-ref\d+/.test(stub.tgt) &&
!/-ref\d+/.test(reqId) &&
stub.tgt.replace(/-ref\d+/,'') == reqId ) {
var tgtElem = document.getElementById(reqId);
if(tgtElem) {
// sync to the ad stub value
tgtElem.id = reqId = stub.tgt;
}
}
if(stub.tgt == reqId) {
try {
var storedAdKey = 'tripads.' + stub.tgt;
if(taStore.has(storedAdKey)) {
tripad = taStore.retrieve(storedAdKey);
break;
} else {
tripad = adSlot.init(stub, {});
break;
}
} catch(e) {
// fail with null tripad
return null;
}
}
}
}
}
// TODO
// if(ta.common.behavior && ta.common.behavior.gutterAd) {
//  var adTgt = ta.id(adStub.tgt);
//  if(adTgt && adTgt.hasClass(ta.common.behavior.gutterAd.adElemClass) && tripad) {
//    tripad.gutterAd = true;
//  }
// }
} catch(e) {
var stubId = (typeof adStub == 'string') ? adStub : adStub.tgt;
taError.record(e, 'unable to get ad for id: ' + stubId );
}
}
return tripad;
}
/**
* Make sure we've loaded the API and are ready to display ads
*
* @private
*/
function _checkForAPILoaded() {
if(!_initialized) {
// Inject the DoubleClick API scripts
dblClick.init(false, _postRenderAdProcessing);
// ADS-3382 - Load JS AMD to track display events in holistic tracking.
if(taStore.retrieve('ads.holisticTracking') === true) {
require(['trjs!retargeting/listeners/desktop-display-adview'], function(adViewListener) {
var options = ta.retrieve('ads.adTracking') || {};
adViewListener(options);
});
}
_initialized = true;
_subscribeToEvents();
}
}
/**
* Initialize the DoubleClick API
*
* API-dependent functions are queued via googletag.cmd
*
* @private
*/
function _initDoubleClick() {
// needed until we update the collapser JS
taStore.store('ads.gptEnabled', true);
// check for ad targets
var targets = $('.gptAd');
if(targets.length > 0) {
// Inject the DoubleClick API scripts
// This can also happen later via queueForInjection, for ajax ads, etc.
_checkForAPILoaded();
googletag.cmd.push(function(){
// inject viewable pageload ads and defer the rest
_injectViewable();
});
}
}
/**
* This method is for queueing/refreshing any ads not handled during pageLoad (initDoubleClick)
*
* This is the goto method for ads in lightboxes, hidden layers etc.
* If you are refreshing all the ads on the page, fire an event to trigger refreshAllAdsPolitely instead.
*
* @param {Object} data
*
* @private
*/
function _queueForInjection(data) {
var elemIds = data && data.elemIds;
var bNewContext =  data && !!data.isNewContext;
if(!elemIds) {
return;
}
// Make sure DoubleClick API is loaded
_checkForAPILoaded();
googletag.cmd.push(function(){
elemIds.forEach(function(elemId){
var elem = document.getElementById(elemId);
if(elem) {
var tripad;
var ajaxServlet = elem.getAttribute("data-ajax-servlet");
if(ajaxServlet) {
tripad = _getAd(elemId, ajaxServlet);
} else {
tripad = _getAd(elemId);
}
if(tripad) {
tripad.injectWhenViewable(bNewContext);
}
}
});
});
}
/**
* Making this available for existing photolightboxes, preroll video etc.
*
* Map the legacy method to the new event-based method
*
* @param {Array} elemIds
* @param {Boolean} bNewContext
*
* There are about a dozen usages of the namespaced method.
*
* @private
*/
function deprecatedQueueForInjection(elemIds, bNewContext) {
var data = {};
data.elemIds = elemIds;
data.isNewContext = bNewContext;
_queueForInjection(data);
}
/**
* Ajax ads have their own targeting and validation.
* For the /MapAdsAjax servlet we use the following JSON:
*  targeting: taStore.retrieve('ads.mapadajax.pageTargeting');
*  stubs: taStore.retrieve('ads.mapadajax.adStubs');
*
* Making this available for existing photolightboxes, preroll video etc.
*
* There are ~11 usages of the namespaced method.
*
* @param {String} - sServlet: the ajax servlet
* @param {String} - selector: for ads to inject
* @param {Boolean} - bNewContext: true for new correlator
*
* @private
*/
function deprecatedInjectAjaxAds(sServlet, selector, bNewContext) {
// Make sure DoubleClick API is loaded
_checkForAPILoaded();
googletag.cmd.push( function(){
if(typeof sServlet == "string") {
// .ads.mapadajax
var servletKey = 'ads.' + sServlet.toLowerCase();
var stubs = taStore.retrieve(servletKey + '.adStubs');
var targeting = taStore.retrieve(servletKey + '.pageTargeting');
var adTargets = $(selector);
if(stubs && stubs.length && adTargets.length) {
adTargets.each(function(idx, adTarget) {
var adStub = false;
for(var i=0; i < stubs.length; i++ ) {
var stub = stubs[i];
if( stub && stub.tgt ) {
/**
*  This is where it gets messy...
*  If we are updating a page-load ad via ajax
*  The ad id in ajax response ( ad stub JSON ) will not match the
*  ad id on the page, so we will compromise by using
*  the ajax ad stub that matches the size of the target div
*  This allows us to update gpt-ad-728x90 using the ajax stub for gpt-ad-728x90-mapadajax
*/
var slices = stub.tgt.split('-');
var adIdToMatch = slices.slice(0,slices.length-1).join('-');
if(adTarget.id.indexOf(adIdToMatch) > -1) {
// here we update the target div id
stub.tgt = adTarget.id;
adStub = stub;
break;
}
}
}
if(adStub) {
try {
// create or retrieve ad slot
var tripAd = _getAd(adStub);
if(tripAd) {
// add the ajax targeting
if(targeting) {
tripAd.addTargeting(targeting);
}
tripAd.injectWhenViewable(bNewContext);
}
} catch(e) {
taError.record(e, 'unable to inject ajax ad for: ' + adStub.tgt);
}
}
});
}
}
});
}
/**
* Making this available for existing photolightboxes, preroll video etc.
*
* There are ~11 usages of the namespaced method.
*
* @param {String} - sServlet: the ajax servlet
* @param {String} - selector: for ads to inject
* @param {Boolean} - bNewContext: true for new correlator
*
* @public
*/
_exports.injectAjaxAds = deprecatedInjectAjaxAds;
/**
* Making this available for existing photolightboxes, preroll video etc.
*
* There are ~9 usages of the namespaced methiod.
*
* @param {Array} - of element Ids
*
* @public
*/
_exports.queueForInjection = deprecatedQueueForInjection;
/**
* This is currently exposed for use by AdDebug, and also by some expandable ads.
*
* @public
*/
_exports.disableRefresh = function() {
_enableRefresh = false;
};
/**
* This function is called by trafficked ad content ( TA's 1x1 collapser pixel )
* The collapser displays as the ad of last resort and collapses the ad div
* We do this to maintain accurate impression forecasting data.
*
* This could also be refqctored to use fireEvent
*
* @param {Element} frameElem - the DoubleClick-created iframe
*
* @public
*/
_exports.collapseAd = function(frameElem) {
if(frameElem) {
$(frameElem.parentNode).parent('.gptAd').addClass('taEmpty');
}
};
nsExporter.exportTo(_exports, 'ta.common.ads');
taEvent.queueForLoad( _initDoubleClick, 'init cpm ads');
return _exports;
});
});require(['ta/p13n/placements','$prp/enable_cpm_content/handlers'], function(placements, impl) {
window.ta.plc_enable_cpm_content_0_handlers = placements.load('enable_cpm_content','handlers.js', { 'name': 'enable_cpm_content', 'occurrence': 0, 'id': 'taplc_enable_cpm_content_0', 'location_id': 186338, 'servletClass': 'com.TripResearch.servlet.forums2.ShowTopicServlet', 'servletName': 'ShowTopic', 'modules': ["handlers"], 'params': {}, 'data': {}});});
require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(prwidgets) {
prwidgets.initWidgets(document);
});
